I have not strayed since.

I refuse to use an uber or lyft simply because of the impeccable service Mike and his team provides. I love their SUVs, usually Tahoe sized and above. Always clean inside, and it smells amazing!

Whoever comes to pick you up from home/airport will help you with your bags, which I truly appreciate as I am not as physically capable as I used to be in my youth.

The staff appearance is professional, usually in either a full suit or business casual -- more on the business side. Their attitudes and friendliness go a long way. I appreciate every ride they have ever given me.

You can't go wrong with Gold Coast. They have never left me stranded, no matter what time of the day I need to be picked up. I think the latest/earliest time once was when I arrived into San Diego at 3:00 AM! Mike always makes sure that either he or another one of his drivers is there to take you home safely.

If for whatever reason, the driver gets held up, they will let you know and communicate it to you ASAP via text or phone call. One time a driver of mine got held up by traffic. No big deal, I was able to kill time by smoking a cigarette and stretching my legs after a long flight.

They are very accommodating to the fact that stuff happens! If your flight gets delayed, just text Mike ASAP and he will make sure that there is someone there to get you.

<user>117408810981407511679<//user>< text>
I wanted to take this opportunity to thank the proprietors of Rogue Knight for a number of reasons. I've been bouncing back and forth between local game stores for years, and every place I've tried to settle into has ended up not working out. Sometimes the staff are dismissive or aloof. Sometimes the clientele are elitist. Some stores offer a limited selection or uncompetitive prices. Some stores are a perfect storm of all of these things.

Rogue Knight is special. From the moment I walked in that first time, I was greeted warmly and genuinely. The staff wasn't bothered by my presence. They approached me, engaged with me and helped me find my way around. They took an active interest in what I was looking for and proved themselves extremely knowledgeable about everything they carry.

The people who frequent Rogue Knight are as friendly as the staff. I've met and played with complete strangers, exchanged contact information gladly and even gotten a taste of new games and hobbies.

Even as a new store, Rogue Knight's selection is considerable. The store is neat and cleanly organized. It's easy to shop and even easier to find something worth buying. Of particular note for rpg fans like me is an impressive array of D&D 5e and Pathfinder products. And if you can't find what you're looking for, the staff is willing to either try hunting it down and ordering it or recommending something very close. All of this with competitive prices to boot.

Add all of this together and throw in generous operating hours, an open and clean floor-space and plenty of demo games to pass the time and you do have a perfect storm; the kind of perfect storm that keeps you coming back and making new friends, diving into new hobbies and creating great new memories.

Once again, thank you guys so much. Consider this the endorsement of someone who had long ago given up finding a game store that would work. I cannot begin to express how nice it is to have finally found that place.

Thanks guys.</text>

< text>
It was a nice park, fairly maintained, from a distance you see plush green grass, nice play ground equipment, with wooded bedding, nice big shade tress, perfect for an afternoon walk or play, wrap around sidewalks, basketball courts. What you can't see is the trash and other disturbing items along the walk around the park... When you start walking through the grass you find containers with melted holes and a straw mechanism twisted through it, razor blades by tress, dirty pooped boxers by the wall, pickle container trash, ropes around trees, bums at tables with all their belongings, bums laying in the grass, people dropped off in the parking lot meeting up with the bums in the grass... Bums asking if we bread our dogs, and barking at them... We walked 2 laps and left... I would recommend unless you just wanted to pee your dog real quick, like we did. Will not return, its sad what parks have become, because theres no proper place for the homless bums to stay...< /text>

This is the best bakery in Merced, Mexican or otherwise. It's not easy to find, they could probably do with a new sign but they are always busy so I guess they don't need it. The baked goods are awesome. I also like the hot food that I have tried so far. The tamales have a perfect meat:masa ratio and everything always tastes fresh which is always a good thing. I am sure that those bigger mercado type stores have their benefits but I know where to go to get quality and taste. The prices are even better too!</text>

<Text>I was lucky enough to be at Folded Hills this past weekend for opening day of their new Homestead Winery and Tasting Room. OMG what a cool place this is!! They took the original farmers house - where they used to make pre prohibition wine btw - and completely renovated it while somehow still letting the history of the place shine through. Wow! This place is seriously gorgeous. I had already been to their Montecito Tasting Room (also awesome) so I knew I loved all of the wines, but this place really blew me away. We meant to pop in for an hour or so, and ended up staying all day! Bring a picnic lunch...you won't want to leave. Lots of great areas to hang, inside and out, and enjoy a wine tasting...or in our case a few bottles...of their award winning Lilly Ros√© and my favorite, August White! They also have backgammon...bocce ball...cornhole...and even yard farkle!! I'm in heaven. Whoever designed this place is a genius. Grab some bottles to go and don't forget a trucker hat! I've gotten asked like ten times already where I got it! I'll be back soon, I loved it all so much I joined the wine club! Can't wait for the private wine club party this fall!! HIGHLY RECOMMEND!< /Text>< pics>
